      <b data-is-speakable>NPR - Breaking News, Analysis, Music, Arts & Podcasts</b>   <b data-is-speakable>Top stories in the U.S. and world news, politics, health, science, business, music, arts and culture. Nonprofit journalism with a mission. This is NPR.</b>

      <section id="main-section"><a id="mainContent"></a><div id="experimentWrap">
      <style type="text/css">article.experimentVariant { display: none; } 
</style>   <script type='text/javascript'>
    // helper functions
    var generateIdForExperimentVariant = function(experimentId, variantId) {
      return 'article.experimentVariant#story' + experimentId.toString() +  variantId.toString();
    };

    NPR.serverVars.experimentMetrics = [];
    var experimentStyles = '';

    var experimentList = NPR.serverVars.experiments || [];
    experimentList.forEach(function(experiment) {
        var experimentId = experiment.id;
        var experimentStoryId = experiment.storyId;
        var variants = experiment.variants;

        if (!variants || !variants.length) {
            return;
        }

        var randomValue =  Math.random();

        // select a variant weighted on the frequencies in the variant metadata
        // the frequencies are between 0 and 1, and the sum of the frequencies add up to 1
        var weightedSum = 0;
        var variantId = variants[0].id;
        var pickedOne = false;
        for (var index = 0; index < variants.length; index++) {
            var variant = variants[index];
            weightedSum += parseFloat(variant.freq);

            if (!pickedOne && randomValue <= weightedSum) {
                variantId = variant.id;
                pickedOne = true;
                experimentStyles += generateIdForExperimentVariant(experimentStoryId, variant.id) + ' { display:block;} \n';
            }
            else {
                experimentStyles += generateIdForExperimentVariant(experimentStoryId, variant.id) + ' { display:none;} \n';
            }
        }
        // store info for use by Google Analytics later
        NPR.serverVars.experimentMetrics.push([experimentId,variantId,experimentStoryId]);

        // https://www.admonsters.com/blog/pixel-delivery-best-practices
        // http://stackoverflow.com/a/22419389
        (new Image()).src = NPR.serverVars.experimentTrackingHost + '/abtesting/experiments/' + experimentId + '/variants/' +  variantId + '/impression.gif';
    });

    // attaching the live click handler
    document.addEventListener('click', function (event) {
        if (NPR.serverVars.experimentMetrics && NPR.serverVars.experimentMetrics.constructor === Array) {
            NPR.serverVars.experimentMetrics.forEach(function (experimentVariant) {
                var experimentId = experimentVariant[0];
                var variantId = experimentVariant[1];
                var experimentStoryId = experimentVariant[2];

                var idToSearchFor = 'story' + experimentStoryId + variantId;
                var el = event.target
                        , found;

                while (el && !(found = el.id === idToSearchFor)) {
                    el = el.parentElement;
                }

                if (found) {
                    (new Image()).src = NPR.serverVars.experimentTrackingHost + '/abtesting/experiments/' + experimentId + '/variants/' + variantId + '/click.gif';
                }
            });
        }
    });

    var styleDiv = document.createElement('div');
    styleDiv.innerHTML = '<style>' + experimentStyles + '</style>';
    document.getElementById('experimentWrap').appendChild(styleDiv.childNodes[0]);
</script>
</div>

<!-- END ID="EXPERIMENTWRAP" -->

                    <h2 class="slug">
                        <a href="https://www.npr.org/sections/national/"  data-metrics-ga4='{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;homepage_curation_click&quot;,&quot;category&quot;:&quot;recirculation&quot;,&quot;clickPosition&quot;:&quot;4-L&quot;,&quot;clickType&quot;:&quot;section slug&quot;,&quot;clickUrl&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/www.npr.org\/sections\/national\/&quot;}' ">
                        National
                        </a>
                    </h2>
                </div>

            <a href="https://www.npr.org/2025/06/03/nx-s1-5421353/trump-officials-alaska-oil-field-drilling"  data-metrics-ga4='{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;homepage_curation_click&quot;,&quot;category&quot;:&quot;recirculation&quot;,&quot;clickPosition&quot;:&quot;4-L&quot;,&quot;clickType&quot;:&quot;curated story&quot;,&quot;clickUrl&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/www.npr.org\/2025\/06\/03\/nx-s1-5421353\/trump-officials-alaska-oil-field-drilling&quot;}' ">
            <h3 class="title">Top Trump officials visit prolific Alaska oil field amid push to expand drilling</h3>
            </a>


            <a href="https://www.npr.org/2025/06/03/nx-s1-5421353/trump-officials-alaska-oil-field-drilling"  data-metrics-ga4='{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;homepage_curation_click&quot;,&quot;category&quot;:&quot;recirculation&quot;,&quot;clickPosition&quot;:&quot;4-L&quot;,&quot;clickType&quot;:&quot;curated story&quot;,&quot;clickUrl&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/www.npr.org\/2025\/06\/03\/nx-s1-5421353\/trump-officials-alaska-oil-field-drilling&quot;}' }'>
                <p class="teaser">President Donald Trump wants to double the amount of oil coursing through Alaska's vast pipeline system and build a massive natural gas project, a top administration official said Monday.</p>
            </a>

                    <h2 class="slug">
                        <a href="https://www.npr.org/sections/science/"  data-metrics-ga4='{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;homepage_curation_click&quot;,&quot;category&quot;:&quot;recirculation&quot;,&quot;clickPosition&quot;:&quot;6-L&quot;,&quot;clickType&quot;:&quot;section slug&quot;,&quot;clickUrl&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/www.npr.org\/sections\/science\/&quot;}' ">
                        Science
                        </a>
                    </h2>
                </div>

            <a href="https://www.npr.org/2025/06/02/nx-s1-5407527/clownfish-climate-change-heat-stress"  data-metrics-ga4='{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;homepage_curation_click&quot;,&quot;category&quot;:&quot;recirculation&quot;,&quot;clickPosition&quot;:&quot;6-L&quot;,&quot;clickType&quot;:&quot;curated story&quot;,&quot;clickUrl&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/www.npr.org\/2025\/06\/02\/nx-s1-5407527\/clownfish-climate-change-heat-stress&quot;}' ">
            <h3 class="title">Some clownfish are shrinking, according to a new study. Here's why</h3>
            </a>


            <a href="https://www.npr.org/2025/06/02/nx-s1-5407527/clownfish-climate-change-heat-stress"  data-metrics-ga4='{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;homepage_curation_click&quot;,&quot;category&quot;:&quot;recirculation&quot;,&quot;clickPosition&quot;:&quot;6-L&quot;,&quot;clickType&quot;:&quot;curated story&quot;,&quot;clickUrl&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/www.npr.org\/2025\/06\/02\/nx-s1-5407527\/clownfish-climate-change-heat-stress&quot;}' }'>
                <p class="teaser">Clownfish in Papua New Guinea are temporarily shrinking in response to heat stress caused by climate change, a new study found. Here's how that might help them deal with warmer water temps.</p>
            </a>
        </div> <!-- /.story-text -->

                Rebecca González-Ramos runs Immigration and Customs Enforcement's intelligence office — known as Homeland Security Investigations — in San Juan, PR. Her mandate under President Trump, she said, is to find every deportable immigrant in Puerto Rico and the U.S. Virgin Islands.

                    Adrian Florido/NPR

                        Immigration
                        </a>
                    </h2>
                </div>

            <a href="https://www.npr.org/2025/06/02/nx-s1-5419588/finding-every-deportable-immigrant-inside-ices-puerto-rico-operation"  data-metrics-ga4='{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;homepage_curation_click&quot;,&quot;category&quot;:&quot;recirculation&quot;,&quot;clickPosition&quot;:&quot;8-L&quot;,&quot;clickType&quot;:&quot;curated story&quot;,&quot;clickUrl&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/www.npr.org\/2025\/06\/02\/nx-s1-5419588\/finding-every-deportable-immigrant-inside-ices-puerto-rico-operation&quot;}' ">
            <h3 class="title">Raids and revenge tips: Inside ICE's Puerto Rico deportation operation</h3>
            </a>


            <a href="https://www.npr.org/2025/06/02/nx-s1-5419588/finding-every-deportable-immigrant-inside-ices-puerto-rico-operation"  data-metrics-ga4='{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;homepage_curation_click&quot;,&quot;category&quot;:&quot;recirculation&quot;,&quot;clickPosition&quot;:&quot;8-L&quot;,&quot;clickType&quot;:&quot;curated story&quot;,&quot;clickUrl&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/www.npr.org\/2025\/06\/02\/nx-s1-5419588\/finding-every-deportable-immigrant-inside-ices-puerto-rico-operation&quot;}' }'>
                <p class="teaser">Rebecca González runs one of ICE's local domestic intelligence offices. She told NPR how her agents are tracking down immigrants in Puerto Rico to deliver on President Trump's mass deportation promise.</p>

                    <h2 class="slug">
                        <a href="https://www.npr.org/sections/science/"  data-metrics-ga4='{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;homepage_curation_click&quot;,&quot;category&quot;:&quot;recirculation&quot;,&quot;clickPosition&quot;:&quot;12-XL&quot;,&quot;clickType&quot;:&quot;section slug&quot;,&quot;clickUrl&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/www.npr.org\/sections\/science\/&quot;}' >
                        Science
                        </a>
                    </h2>

            <a href="https://www.npr.org/2025/06/02/nx-s1-5419557/these-researchers-think-the-sludge-in-your-home-may-help-save-the-planet"  data-metrics-ga4='{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;homepage_curation_click&quot;,&quot;category&quot;:&quot;recirculation&quot;,&quot;clickPosition&quot;:&quot;12-XL&quot;,&quot;clickType&quot;:&quot;curated story&quot;,&quot;clickUrl&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/www.npr.org\/2025\/06\/02\/nx-s1-5419557\/these-researchers-think-the-sludge-in-your-home-may-help-save-the-planet&quot;}' >
            <h3 class="title">These researchers think the sludge in your home may help save the planet</h3>
            </a>


            <a href="https://www.npr.org/2025/06/02/nx-s1-5419557/these-researchers-think-the-sludge-in-your-home-may-help-save-the-planet"  data-metrics-ga4='{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;homepage_curation_click&quot;,&quot;category&quot;:&quot;recirculation&quot;,&quot;clickPosition&quot;:&quot;12-XL&quot;,&quot;clickType&quot;:&quot;curated story&quot;,&quot;clickUrl&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/www.npr.org\/2025\/06\/02\/nx-s1-5419557\/these-researchers-think-the-sludge-in-your-home-may-help-save-the-planet&quot;}' >
                <p class="teaser">What if the solutions to some of Earth's biggest problems could be found in some of its smallest creatures? That bet has led a team of researchers to places both remote and — lately — rather familiar.</p>
            </a>
        </div> <!-- /.story-text -->

            <h3 class="title">Tariffs complicate the Switch 2 launch, says Nintendo of America president</h3>
            </a>


            <a href="https://www.npr.org/2025/04/07/nx-s1-5349650/trump-tariffs-nintendo-switch-2-doug-bowser"  data-metrics-ga4='{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;homepage_curation_click&quot;,&quot;category&quot;:&quot;recirculation&quot;,&quot;clickPosition&quot;:&quot;15-L&quot;,&quot;clickType&quot;:&quot;curated story&quot;,&quot;clickUrl&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/www.npr.org\/2025\/04\/07\/nx-s1-5349650\/trump-tariffs-nintendo-switch-2-doug-bowser&quot;}' }'>
                <p class="teaser">Some retailers appear to be cancelling preorders for the Nintendo Switch 2 ahead of the console's launch June 5. Nintendo of America President Doug Bowser spoke to us about how an ongoing trade war is impacting the Switch 2's release.</p>
            </a>
        </div> <!-- /.story-text -->

            <h3 class="title">Trump's $5 million Gold Card offers the rich a fast lane to residency</h3>

                        Music Interviews
                        </a>
                    </h2>

            <a href="https://www.npr.org/2025/06/02/nx-s1-5348896/simone-dinnerstein-performance-anxiety-complicite"  data-metrics-ga4='{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;homepage_curation_click&quot;,&quot;category&quot;:&quot;recirculation&quot;,&quot;clickPosition&quot;:&quot;18-L&quot;,&quot;clickType&quot;:&quot;curated story&quot;,&quot;clickUrl&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/www.npr.org\/2025\/06\/02\/nx-s1-5348896\/simone-dinnerstein-performance-anxiety-complicite&quot;}' ">
            <h3 class="title">How the iPad cured a top pianist's stage fright</h3>
            </a>


            <a href="https://www.npr.org/2025/06/02/nx-s1-5348896/simone-dinnerstein-performance-anxiety-complicite"  data-metrics-ga4='{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;homepage_curation_click&quot;,&quot;category&quot;:&quot;recirculation&quot;,&quot;clickPosition&quot;:&quot;18-L&quot;,&quot;clickType&quot;:&quot;curated story&quot;,&quot;clickUrl&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/www.npr.org\/2025\/06\/02\/nx-s1-5348896\/simone-dinnerstein-performance-anxiety-complicite&quot;}' }'>
                <p class="teaser">Anxiety and panic attacks crippled pianist Simone Dinnerstein on stage, despite a stellar career. She shares how one common device helped her overcome the fear.</p>

                    <h2 class="slug">
                        <a href="https://www.npr.org/series/1176326550/living-better"  data-metrics-ga4='{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;homepage_curation_click&quot;,&quot;category&quot;:&quot;recirculation&quot;,&quot;clickPosition&quot;:&quot;19-L&quot;,&quot;clickType&quot;:&quot;section slug&quot;,&quot;clickUrl&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/www.npr.org\/series\/1176326550\/living-better&quot;}' ">
                        Living Better
                        </a>
                    </h2>
                </div>

            <a href="https://www.npr.org/2025/06/02/nx-s1-5398375/beef-tallow-balm-natural-skincare-tiktok"  data-metrics-ga4='{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;homepage_curation_click&quot;,&quot;category&quot;:&quot;recirculation&quot;,&quot;clickPosition&quot;:&quot;19-L&quot;,&quot;clickType&quot;:&quot;curated story&quot;,&quot;clickUrl&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/www.npr.org\/2025\/06\/02\/nx-s1-5398375\/beef-tallow-balm-natural-skincare-tiktok&quot;}' ">
            <h3 class="title">Miracle balm or cow pie? What's behind the beef tallow skincare trend</h3>
            </a>


            <a href="https://www.npr.org/2025/06/02/nx-s1-5398375/beef-tallow-balm-natural-skincare-tiktok"  data-metrics-ga4='{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;homepage_curation_click&quot;,&quot;category&quot;:&quot;recirculation&quot;,&quot;clickPosition&quot;:&quot;19-L&quot;,&quot;clickType&quot;:&quot;curated story&quot;,&quot;clickUrl&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/www.npr.org\/2025\/06\/02\/nx-s1-5398375\/beef-tallow-balm-natural-skincare-tiktok&quot;}' }'>
                <p class="teaser">Rendered beef fat is having a moment as a viral skincare trend. TikTok influencers claim this 'natural' product is a complexion panacea. But is it? We asked skincare experts.</p>
            </a>
        </div> <!-- /.story-text -->

            <h3 class="title">With 'I Love Lucy' and beyond, Desi Arnaz helped shaped TV as we know it</h3>
            </a>


            <a href="https://www.npr.org/2025/06/02/nx-s1-5417932/i-love-lucy-desi-arnaz-lucille-ball-todd-purdum"  data-metrics-ga4='{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;homepage_curation_click&quot;,&quot;category&quot;:&quot;recirculation&quot;,&quot;clickPosition&quot;:&quot;20-XL&quot;,&quot;clickType&quot;:&quot;curated story&quot;,&quot;clickUrl&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/www.npr.org\/2025\/06\/02\/nx-s1-5417932\/i-love-lucy-desi-arnaz-lucille-ball-todd-purdum&quot;}' >
                <p class="teaser">The success of I Love Lucy is often credited to Lucille Ball's comedic talent, but biographer Todd Purdum says Arnaz was more than just "second banana" to Lucy. He also helped shape the modern sitcom.</p>
            </a>
        </div> <!-- /.story-text -->

        <div class="story-text">

            <a href="https://one.npr.org/i/1263527125:1269403377"  data-metrics-ga4='{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;homepage_curation_click&quot;,&quot;category&quot;:&quot;recirculation&quot;,&quot;clickPosition&quot;:&quot;25-L&quot;,&quot;clickType&quot;:&quot;curated story&quot;,&quot;clickUrl&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/one.npr.org\/i\/1263527125:1269403377&quot;}' ">
            <h3 class="title">Podcast: Canada hates us, but it's not all Trump's fault</h3>
            </a>


            <a href="https://one.npr.org/i/1263527125:1269403377"  data-metrics-ga4='{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;homepage_curation_click&quot;,&quot;category&quot;:&quot;recirculation&quot;,&quot;clickPosition&quot;:&quot;25-L&quot;,&quot;clickType&quot;:&quot;curated story&quot;,&quot;clickUrl&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/one.npr.org\/i\/1263527125:1269403377&quot;}' }'>
                <p class="teaser">As of April, two-thirds of Canadians considered the U.S. to be "unfriendly" or an "enemy," and 61% say they have started boycotting U.S. companies. But Canadian views of the U.S. have been trending down for decades.</p>
            </a>

            <h3 class="title">Los Tigres del Norte share the pride of selling out Madison Square Garden with their fans</h3>
            </a>


            <a href="https://www.npr.org/2025/06/02/nx-s1-5408615/los-tigres-del-norte-madison-square-garden-show"  data-metrics-ga4='{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;homepage_curation_click&quot;,&quot;category&quot;:&quot;recirculation&quot;,&quot;clickPosition&quot;:&quot;27-L&quot;,&quot;clickType&quot;:&quot;curated story&quot;,&quot;clickUrl&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/www.npr.org\/2025\/06\/02\/nx-s1-5408615\/los-tigres-del-norte-madison-square-garden-show&quot;}' }'>
                <p class="teaser">Los Tigres del Norte has played almost every single place in the country — from armories to rodeos, in big cities and small towns. But they've never played Madison Square Garden.</p>
            </a>

                        <article class="post-type-simple volume-high has-audio has-image has-status" id="story">
        <b class="status">Pride Month</b>

    <div class="story-wrap">

                <div class="slug-wrap">

                    <h2 class="slug">
                        <a href="https://www.npr.org/series/736403088/50-years-after-stonewall"  data-metrics-ga4='{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;homepage_curation_click&quot;,&quot;category&quot;:&quot;recirculation&quot;,&quot;clickPosition&quot;:&quot;28.1-XL&quot;,&quot;clickType&quot;:&quot;section slug&quot;,&quot;clickUrl&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/www.npr.org\/series\/736403088\/50-years-after-stonewall&quot;}' >
                        50 Years After Stonewall
                        </a>
                    </h2>
                </div>

            <a href="https://www.npr.org/2019/06/28/733500331/why-we-remember-stonewall"  data-metrics-ga4='{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;homepage_curation_click&quot;,&quot;category&quot;:&quot;recirculation&quot;,&quot;clickPosition&quot;:&quot;28.1-XL&quot;,&quot;clickType&quot;:&quot;curated story&quot;,&quot;clickUrl&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/www.npr.org\/2019\/06\/28\/733500331\/why-we-remember-stonewall&quot;}' >
            <h3 class="title">Why we remember Stonewall </h3>
            </a>


            <a href="https://www.npr.org/2019/06/28/733500331/why-we-remember-stonewall"  data-metrics-ga4='{&quot;action&quot;:&quot;homepage_curation_click&quot;,&quot;category&quot;:&quot;recirculation&quot;,&quot;clickPosition&quot;:&quot;28.1-XL&quot;,&quot;clickType&quot;:&quot;curated story&quot;,&quot;clickUrl&quot;:&quot;https:\/\/www.npr.org\/2019\/06\/28\/733500331\/why-we-remember-stonewall&quot;}' >
                <p class="teaser">The Stonewall Inn is a sacred place for many in the LGBTQ community. In 1969, a raid and series of riots outside the New York City bar helped launch a civil rights movement.</p>
            </a>
        </div> <!-- /.story-text -->

<div class="credit-caption">
    <div class="caption-wrap">
        <div class="caption" aria-label="Image caption">
            <p>
                "Pronouns are basically how we identify ourselves apart from our name. It's how someone refers to you in conversation," says Mary Emily O'Hara, a communications officer at GLAAD. "And when you're speaking to people, it's a really simple way to affirm their identity."
                <b class="credit" aria-label="Image credit">
                    
                    Kaz Fantone for NPR
                    
                </b>
